multiple layers:\\n\\n## API Key Validation Middleware\\nThe authentication starts in `pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go` where the `ContextHandler.Middleware` processes each HTTP request by calling `authenticator.Authenticate()`. This middleware initializes the request context and extracts the API key from the Authorization header.\\n\\n## API Key Authentication Client\\nIn `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`, the `APIKey` client implements the `Authenticate` method which:\\n1. Extracts the token from HTTP Authorization header via `getTokenFromRequest()`\\n2. Decodes the token using either modern (`satokengen.Decode`) or legacy (`apikeygen.Decode`) format\\n3. Retrieves the hashed key and looks up the API key in the database via `apiKeyService.GetAPIKeyByHash()`\\n4. Validates the API key using `validateApiKey()` which checks:\\n   - Expiration date (`key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()` returns `errAPIKeyExpired`)\\n   - Revocation status (`key.IsRevoked` returns `errAPIKeyRevoked`)\\n   - Organization membership (`orgID != key.OrgID` returns `errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`)\\n   - Service account association (required for modern keys)\\n\\n## Service Account Token Generation\\nTokens are generated and validated in:\\n- `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go`: Generates service account tokens with format `glSERVICE_ID_SECRET_CHECKSUM` using CRC32 checksums\\n- `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`: Legacy API key format using base64-encoded JSON\\n\\nBoth support `Decode()` and hash validation functions.\\n\\n## Key Expiration Handling\\nAPI key expiration is enforced at multiple levels:\\n1. In `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`, the `validateApiKey()` function checks if `*key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()`\\n2. In `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go`, the `AddAPIKey()` function sets expiration based on `cmd.SecondsToLive`\\n3. In `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/secretscan/service.go`, the `hasExpired()` function checks token expiration before inclusion in secret scanning checks\\n\\n## Scope and Permission Enforcement\\nAfter API key validation, permissions are synced via `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go`:\\n1. The `SyncPermissionsHook` is registered as post-auth hook (priority 120)\\n2. It calls `fetchPermissions()` which retrieves user permissions from the access control service\\n3. Permissions are grouped by action and scope using `accesscontrol.GroupScopesByActionContext()`\\n4. The API key client sets `ClientParams{FetchSyncedUser: true, SyncPermissions: true}` to enable permission syncing\\n\\n## GRPC Authentication\\nFor GRPC endpoints, `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go` provides:\\n1. Token extraction from GRPC Authorization header\\n2. API key validation via `apiKeyService.GetAPIKeyByHash()`\\n3. Service account role verification (must have Admin role)\\n4. Permission fetching via access control service\\n5. Disabled service account detection\\n\\n## Revocation and Secret Scanning\\nIn `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/secretscan/service.go`:\\n1. `CheckTokens()` retrieves active tokens via `filterCheckableTokens()`\\n2. Filters out expired tokens (`hasExpired()`) and revoked tokens (`token.IsRevoked`)\\n3. Checks token hashes against external secret scanning service\\n4. Can automatically revoke leaked tokens via `RevokeServiceAccountToken()`\\n\\n## Database Operations\\nAPI keys are persisted in `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go` with operations:\\n- `GetAPIKeyByHash()`: Core lookup method used during authentication\\n- `GetApiKeyByName()`: Legacy key lookup for old-format keys\\n- `GetAllAPIKeys()`: Retrieve organization's API keys\\n- `AddAPIKey()`: Create new key with expiration validation\\n- `UpdateAPIKeyLastUsedDate()`: Track API key usage\\n\\n## HTTP Middleware\\nIn `pkg/middleware/auth.go`, role-based access control is enforced via:\\n- `RoleAuth()`: Middleware checking user's organization role\\n- `Auth()`: Middleware enforcing authentication requirements\\nThese work with the API key's associated service account role.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6380,"cache_read_input_tokens":95973,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6380},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"3a1e4a18-c7cd-4af0-8121-ae83f3edbb44","uuid":"fb6acaf2-f48c-42ec-b2cf-4d6a05a2631b"}

multiple layers:\\n\\n## API Key Validation Middleware\\nThe authentication starts in `pkg/services/contexthandler/contexthandler.go` where the `ContextHandler.Middleware` processes each HTTP request by calling `authenticator.Authenticate()`. This middleware initializes the request context and extracts the API key from the Authorization header.\\n\\n## API Key Authentication Client\\nIn `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`, the `APIKey` client implements the `Authenticate` method which:\\n1. Extracts the token from HTTP Authorization header via `getTokenFromRequest()`\\n2. Decodes the token using either modern (`satokengen.Decode`) or legacy (`apikeygen.Decode`) format\\n3. Retrieves the hashed key and looks up the API key in the database via `apiKeyService.GetAPIKeyByHash()`\\n4. Validates the API key using `validateApiKey()` which checks:\\n   - Expiration date (`key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()` returns `errAPIKeyExpired`)\\n   - Revocation status (`key.IsRevoked` returns `errAPIKeyRevoked`)\\n   - Organization membership (`orgID != key.OrgID` returns `errAPIKeyOrgMismatch`)\\n   - Service account association (required for modern keys)\\n\\n## Service Account Token Generation\\nTokens are generated and validated in:\\n- `pkg/components/satokengen/tokengen.go`: Generates service account tokens with format `glSERVICE_ID_SECRET_CHECKSUM` using CRC32 checksums\\n- `pkg/components/apikeygen/apikeygen.go`: Legacy API key format using base64-encoded JSON\\n\\nBoth support `Decode()` and hash validation functions.\\n\\n## Key Expiration Handling\\nAPI key expiration is enforced at multiple levels:\\n1. In `pkg/services/authn/clients/api_key.go`, the `validateApiKey()` function checks if `*key.Expires <= time.Now().Unix()`\\n2. In `pkg/services/apikey/apikeyimpl/xorm_store.go`, the `AddAPIKey()` function sets expiration based on `cmd.SecondsToLive`\\n3. In `pkg/services/serviceaccounts/secretscan/service.go`, the `hasExpired()` function checks token expiration before inclusion in secret scanning checks\\n\\n## Scope and Permission Enforcement\\nAfter API key validation, permissions are synced via `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/sync/rbac_sync.go`:\\n1. The `SyncPermissionsHook` is registered as post-auth hook (priority 120)\\n2. It calls `fetchPermissions()` which retrieves user permissions from the access control service\\n3. Permissions are grouped by action and scope using `accesscontrol.GroupScopesByActionContext()`\\n4. The API key client sets `ClientParams{FetchSyncedUser: true, SyncPermissions: true}` to enable permission syncing\\n\\n## GRPC Authentication\\nFor GRPC endpoints, `pkg/services/grpcserver/interceptors/auth.go` provides:\\n1. Token extraction from GRPC Authorization header\\n2. API key validation via `apiKeyService.GetAPIKeyByHash()`\\n3. Service account role verification (must have Admin role)\\n4. Permission fetching via access control service\\n5. Filters out expired tokens (`hasExpired()`) and revoked tokens (`token.IsRevoked`)\\n3. Checks token hashes against external secret scanning service\\n4.
